country_event = {

							1177.EJZ_NEP_influence > 4
						}
					}
					1177 = {
						add_to_variable = {
							EJZ_DSU_influence = 5
							}
						subtract_from_variable = {
							EJZ_NEP_influence = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
	    }	
	}
	}
    }  
}
